-aide moi dans la tache 2Git et documentation=20

je suis youssef sayari 4sae6 a esprit

mon application est spring angular
architecture : microservice=20
 ma tache est gestion de reclamation : en faite il sagit dune application d=
edie aux hotels=20
les type dutilisateur : Visiteur ou admin
a travers ma tache vous pouvez passer des reclamation :
Voici mon controller :=20
@Tag(name =3D "Complaint Management")
@RestController
@AllArgsConstructor
@RequestMapping("/complaint")
public class ComplaintRestController {
    @Autowired
    private final ComplaintService complaintService;

    private final ComplaintSolutionIAService complaintSolutionIAService;

    // CREATE
    @PostMapping("/addComplaint")
    public ResponseEntity&lt;?&gt; createComplaint(
            @Valid @RequestBody Complaint complaint,
            BindingResult result,
            @RequestParam Long userId) {

        if (result.hasErrors()) {
            return buildValidationErrorResponse(result);
        }

        try {
            Complaint createdComplaint =3D complaintService.createComplaint=
(complaint, userId);
            return new ResponseEntity&lt;&gt;(createdComplaint, HttpStatus.=
CREATED);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST)
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "Failed to create complaint",
                            "details", e.getMessage()
                    ));
        }
    }

    // READ
    @GetMapping("/getComplaintById/{id}")
    public ResponseEntity&lt;?&gt; getComplaint(@PathVariable Long id) {
        try {
            Complaint complaint =3D complaintService.getComplaintById(id);
            return ResponseEntity.ok(complaint);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND)
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "Complaint not found",
                            "details", e.getMessage()
                    ));
        }
    }

    @GetMapping("/getAllComplaints")
    public ResponseEntity&lt;?&gt; getAllComplaints() {
        try {
            List&lt;Complaint&gt; complaints =3D complaintService.getAllCom=
plaints();
            return ResponseEntity.ok(complaints);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "Failed to retrieve complaints",
                            "details", e.getMessage()
                    ));
        }
    }
    @GetMapping("/getComplaintsByStatus/{status}")
    public ResponseEntity&lt;?&gt; getComplaintsByStatus(@PathVariable Comp=
laintStatus status) {
        try {
            List&lt;Complaint&gt; complaints =3D complaintService.getCompla=
intsByStatus(status);
            return ResponseEntity.ok(complaints);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "Failed to retrieve complaints by stat=
us",
                            "details", e.getMessage()
                    ));
        }
    }
    @GetMapping("/getComplaintsByUser/{userId}")
    public ResponseEntity&lt;?&gt; getComplaintsByUser(@PathVariable Long u=
serId) {
        try {
            List&lt;Complaint&gt; complaints =3D complaintService.getCompla=
intsByUser(userId);
            return ResponseEntity.ok(complaints);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "Failed to retrieve user complaints",
                            "details", e.getMessage()
                    ));
        }
    }

    // UPDATE
    @PutMapping("/updateComplaint/{id}")
    public ResponseEntity&lt;?&gt; updateComplaint(
            @PathVariable Long id,
            @Valid @RequestBody Complaint complaint,
            BindingResult result) {

        if (result.hasErrors()) {
            // Retournez les erreurs de validation au frontend
            List&lt;String&gt; errors =3D result.getFieldErrors().stream()
                    .map(error -&gt; error.getField() + ": " + error.getDef=
aultMessage())
                    .collect(Collectors.toList());

            return ResponseEntity.badRequest()
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "Validation failed",
                            "details", errors
                    ));
        }

        try {
            Complaint updatedComplaint =3D complaintService.updateComplaint=
(id, complaint);
            return ResponseEntity.ok(updatedComplaint);
        } catch (IllegalArgumentException e) {
            // Gestion sp=C3=A9cifique des erreurs m=C3=A9tier
            return ResponseEntity.badRequest()
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "Business rule violation",
                            "message", e.getMessage()
                    ));
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.internalServerError()
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "Internal server error",
                            "message", e.getMessage()
                    ));
        }
    }

    // DELETE

    @DeleteMapping("/deleteComplaint/{id}")
    public ResponseEntity&lt;Map&lt;String, Object&gt;&gt; deleteComplaint(=
@PathVariable Long id) {
        if (complaintService.getComplaintById(id)=3D=3Dnull) { // V=C3=A9ri=
fication avant suppression
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.NOT_FOUND)
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "R=C3=A9clamation introuvable",
                            "id", id,
                            "details", "Aucune r=C3=A9clamation trouv=C3=A9=
e avec l'ID " + id
                    ));
        }

        try {
            complaintService.deleteComplaint(id);
            return ResponseEntity.ok(Map.of(
                    "message", "La r=C3=A9clamation a =C3=A9t=C3=A9 supprim=
=C3=A9e avec succ=C3=A8s.",
                    "id", id
            ));
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return ResponseEntity.status(HttpStatus.INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR)
                    .body(Map.of(
                            "error", "=C3=89chec de la suppression",
                            "id", id,
                            "details", e.getMessage()
                    ));
        }
    }



    // M=C3=A9thode utilitaire pour g=C3=A9rer les erreurs de validation
    private ResponseEntity&lt;Map&lt;String, Object&gt;&gt; buildValidation=
ErrorResponse(BindingResult result) {
        List&lt;String&gt; errors =3D result.getFieldErrors()
                .stream()
                .map(error -&gt; error.getField() + ": " + error.getDefault=
Message())
                .collect(Collectors.toList());

        return ResponseEntity.badRequest()
                .body(Map.of(
                        "error", "Validation failed",
                        "messages", errors
                ));
    }

            default -&gt; HttpStatus.OK;

  private formatTunisianTime(date: Date): string {

      hour: '2-digit',

private parseDate(dateInput: any): Date {
  if (dateInput instanceof Date) {
    return dateInput;
  }
 =20
  if (Array.isArray(dateInput)) {
    const [year, month, day, hour =3D 0, minute =3D 0, second =3D 0] =3D da=
teInput;
    return new Date(year, month - 1, day, hour, minute, second);
  }
 =20
  if (typeof dateInput =3D=3D=3D 'string') {
    return new Date(dateInput);
  }
 =20
  // Si le format est inconnu, retournez la date actuelle
  console.warn('Format de date non reconnu:', dateInput);
  return new Date();
}
formatDate(dateInput: any): string {
  const date =3D this.parseDate(dateInput);
  return date.toLocaleDateString('fr-FR'); // Format: dd/mm/yyyy
}
confirmDelete(complaintId: number): void {
  Swal.fire({
    title: 'Confirmer la suppression',
    text: '=C3=8Ates-vous s=C3=BBr de vouloir supprimer cette r=C3=A9clamat=
ion?',
    icon: 'warning',
    showCancelButton: true,
    confirmButtonColor: '#3085d6',
    cancelButtonColor: '#d33',
    confirmButtonText: 'Oui, supprimer!',
    cancelButtonText: 'Annuler',
    customClass: {
      popup: 'modern-swal',
      title: 'text-2xl font-bold',
      confirmButton: 'px-4 py-2 bg-red-600 hover:bg-red-700 rounded-lg',
      cancelButton: 'px-4 py-2 bg-gray-200 hover:bg-gray-300 rounded-lg mr-=
3'
    }
  }).then((result) =3D&gt; {
    if (result.isConfirmed) {
      this.deleteComplaint(complaintId);
    }
  });
}

private deleteComplaint(id: number): void {
  // Suppression optimiste
  const complaintToRemove =3D this.complaints.find(c =3D&gt; c.id =3D=3D=3D=
 id);
  if (!complaintToRemove) return; // Si la r=C3=A9clamation n'existe pas da=
ns la liste, rien =C3=A0 faire.

  // Enlever la r=C3=A9clamation de la liste optimiste
  this.complaints =3D this.complaints.filter(c =3D&gt; c.id !=3D=3D id);
  this.updateStatusStats();
  this.totalComplaintsCount--;
 =20
  // Appel au service de suppression
  this.complaintService.deleteComplaint(id).subscribe({
    next: () =3D&gt; {
      // Succes de la suppression
      Swal.fire({
        title: 'Supprim=C3=A9!',
        text: 'La r=C3=A9clamation a =C3=A9t=C3=A9 supprim=C3=A9e avec succ=
=C3=A8s.',
        icon: 'success',
        timer: 2000,
        showConfirmButton: false,
        customClass: {
          popup: 'modern-swal-success'
        }
      });
    },
    error: (err) =3D&gt; {
      // Si erreur, restaurer l'=C3=A9l=C3=A9ment et afficher un message d'=
erreur
      this.complaints.push(complaintToRemove);
      this.updateStatusStats();
      this.totalComplaintsCount++;

      Swal.fire({
        title: 'Erreur!',
        text: 'La suppression a =C3=A9chou=C3=A9: ' + err.message,
        icon: 'error',
        customClass: {
          popup: 'modern-swal-error'
        }
      });
    }
  });
}

/*---------------------------------- PARTIE IA ----------------------------=

// M=C3=A9thode pour consulter l'IA
consultWithAI(complaint: Complaint) {
  this.selectedComplaint =3D complaint;
  this.aiState =3D 'loading';
  this.aiResponse =3D null;
  this.aiError =3D '';

  this.complaintService.getSolutionByComplaint(complaint.id!).subscribe({
    next: (existingSolution) =3D&gt; {
      if (existingSolution) {
        this.isNewSolution =3D false;
        this.mapExistingSolution(existingSolution);
      } else {
        this.isNewSolution =3D true;
        this.generateNewSolution(complaint);
      }
    },
    error: () =3D&gt; this.generateNewSolution(complaint)
  });
}

private mapExistingSolution(solution: ComplaintSolutionIA) {
  this.aiResponse =3D {
    message: solution.analyseReclamation,
    solution: solution.solutionProposee,
    apaisement: solution.compensation,
    delai: '24 heures' // Adaptez selon vos donn=C3=A9es
  };
  this.aiState =3D 'done';
}

private generateNewSolution(complaint: Complaint) {
  this.complaintService.generateAiSolution(
    complaint.category,
    complaint.description
  ).subscribe({
    next: (response) =3D&gt; {
      setTimeout(() =3D&gt; {
        this.aiResponse =3D response;
        this.aiState =3D 'done';
      }, 1500);
    },
    error: (err) =3D&gt; {
      this.aiError =3D err.message || "Erreur lors de l'analyse";
      this.aiState =3D 'error';
    }
  });
}

// M=C3=A9thode pour accepter la solution IA
acceptSolution() {
  if (!this.selectedComplaint?.id || !this.aiResponse || !this.selectedComp=
laint.user) {
    this.resetAI();
    return;
  }

  // Pr=C3=A9parer l'objet solution IA selon le mod=C3=A8le backend
  const solutionIA: ComplaintSolutionIA =3D {
    id: 0, // L'ID sera g=C3=A9n=C3=A9r=C3=A9 c=C3=B4t=C3=A9 serveur
    analyseReclamation: this.aiResponse.message,
    solutionProposee: this.aiResponse.solution,
    compensation: this.aiResponse.apaisement || '',
    complaintId: this.selectedComplaint.id
  };

  // Appeler le service sp=C3=A9cifique pour accepter la solution IA
  this.complaintService.acceptSolutionAndAffectToComplaint(
    this.selectedComplaint.id,
    solutionIA
  ).subscribe({
    next: () =3D&gt; {
      // Cr=C3=A9er un objet Complaint complet avec toutes les propri=C3=A9=
t=C3=A9s requises
      const updatedComplaint: Complaint =3D {
        ...this.selectedComplaint!,
        status: ComplaintStatus.EN_PROGRESSION,
        user: this.selectedComplaint!.user, // Garanti non-undefined gr=C3=
=A2ce =C3=A0 la v=C3=A9rification initiale
        complaintDate: this.selectedComplaint!.complaintDate || new Date(),
        description: this.selectedComplaint!.description || '',
        category: this.selectedComplaint!.category || ComplaintCategories.A=
UTRE,
        resolutionDetails: this.selectedComplaint!.resolutionDetails || nul=
l,
        resolutionDate: this.selectedComplaint!.resolutionDate || null
      };

      // Mettre =C3=A0 jour la r=C3=A9clamation dans la liste
      const index =3D this.complaints.findIndex(c =3D&gt; c.id =3D=3D=3D up=
datedComplaint.id);
      if (index !=3D=3D -1) {
        this.complaints[index] =3D updatedComplaint;
      }

      // Notification de succ=C3=A8s
      Swal.fire({
        title: 'Solution accept=C3=A9e',
        text: 'La solution IA a =C3=A9t=C3=A9 appliqu=C3=A9e avec succ=C3=
=A8s',
        icon: 'success',
        timer: 10000,
        showConfirmButton: false,
        position: 'center',
        customClass: {
          popup: 'modern-swal',
          title: 'text-lg font-bold'
        }
      });

      this.resetAI();
    },
    error: (err) =3D&gt; {
      Swal.fire({
        title: 'Erreur',
        text: '=C3=89chec de l\'application de la solution: ' +=20
              (err.error?.message || err.message || 'Erreur inconnue'),
        icon: 'error',
        timer: 3000
      });
    }
  });
}


requestHumanHelp() {
  // Impl=C3=A9mentez la logique de demande d'aide humaine
  Swal.fire({
    title: 'Demande envoy=C3=A9e',
    text: 'Un membre de notre =C3=A9quipe va prendre en charge votre r=C3=
=A9clamation',
    icon: 'info',
    timer: 10000
  });
 =20
  this.resetAI();
}

resetAI() {
  this.aiState =3D 'idle';
  this.selectedComplaint =3D null;
  this.aiResponse =3D null;
  this.aiError =3D '';
}

ss=3D"e1675d8b"><div class=3D"_9ecc93a"></div><p class=3D"ba94db8a">Okay, l=
et me try to help Youssef with his Git and documentation task. He mentioned=
 he's working on a microservice application using Spring and Angular for ho=
tel complaint management. The task is part of his project for school, and h=
e needs to improve his Git usage and documentation to meet the grading crit=
eria.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">First, looking at =
the requirements for the Git section: regular commits, good project structu=
re, and a consistent project description. He needs to structure his Git rep=
ository properly. Since it's a microservice architecture, each service (lik=
e the complaint service, Eureka server, API Gateway) should probably be in =
separate directories. Maybe a parent Maven project with submodules? That's =
a common structure. He should have folders for each microservice, the Angul=
ar frontend, and possibly a root directory for common configurations or scr=
ipts.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">Next, regular comm=
its. He should make sure his commit history shows incremental progress. May=
be he's been working without committing much yet. Advise him to commit each=
 feature or logical change separately. For example, one commit for setting =
up Eureka, another for the Gateway, another for the complaint service, etc.=
 Each commit message should be clear and descriptive, following conventions=
 like starting with a verb (e.g., "feat: add complaint creation endpoint").=
</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">Documentation: He needs=
 a README.md file that explains the project. The README should have an over=
view of the project, the technologies used, how to set it up, the architect=
ure diagram, API documentation, and any other relevant info. Since he's usi=
ng Spring Boot, maybe include how to run the services, any environment vari=
ables needed, database setup. For the Angular part, how to run the frontend=
.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">Also, maybe include Sw=
agger for API documentation. In his Spring Boot app, adding SpringDoc OpenA=
PI could automatically generate API docs, which he can link in the README. =
That would be a nice touch for the documentation part.</p><p class=3D"ba94d=
b8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">For Git structure, maybe suggest something l=
ike:</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">- root/</p><p class=
=3D"ba94db8a">- eureka-server/</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">- api-gateway/</p><=
p class=3D"ba94db8a">- complaint-service/</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">- fronte=
nd/</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">- README.md</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">- .gitign=
ore</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">Each service is a se=
parate module. The frontend is in its own directory. The .gitignore should =
cover both Java and Angular related files (target/, node_modules/, etc.)</p=
><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">He might also need to incl=
ude a Postman collection or OpenAPI spec file as part of the documentation.=
 If he's using a database, maybe include the schema or migration scripts.</=
p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">Another point is branchin=
g strategy. If he's working alone, maybe he's using main/master branch dire=
ctly, but it's better to use feature branches and merge them via pull reque=
sts for better history. But since it's an individual project, maybe that's =
optional unless specified.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8=
a">For the project description in the README, he should explain the purpose=
 of the application, the user roles (Visitor and Admin), the main features =
(create complaint, view status, AI solution generation), the architecture (=
microservices with Eureka and Gateway), and technologies used (Spring Boot,=
 Angular, MySQL/H2?, Mistral AI for solutions).</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></=
p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">He should also include setup instructions: how to c=
lone the repo, run each service, configure the database, run the frontend. =
Maybe add a section on testing, how to access Eureka dashboard, the API Gat=
eway routes, etc.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">Potent=
ial mistakes he might have made: not committing regularly, having a messy p=
roject structure without clear separation of services, missing or minimal R=
EADME. So, guiding him to organize the repo, write a comprehensive README, =
and make meaningful commits.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94d=
b8a">I should also remind him to check his .gitignore to avoid committing u=
nnecessary files like build directories, IDE files, environment secrets. Th=
at's a common issue.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">Add=
itionally, for the Git part, maybe suggest using tags for versions, especia=
lly if there are releases or milestones. But that might be beyond the curre=
nt scope.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">In summary, th=
e steps for Youssef would be:</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a"></p><p class=3D"ba94=
db8a">1. Reorganize the project structure into clear modules.</p><p class=

</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">3. Commit each module/feature with clear messages=
.</p><p class=3D"ba94db8a">4. Set up proper .gitignore.</p><p class=3D"ba94=

### 4. .gitignore
Ajoutez ces =C3=A9l=C3=A9ments :</pre></div><h1>Java</h1><p>target/<br>*.ja=

### 5. Valeur Ajout=C3=A9e Documentation
- Ajoutez un dossier `docs/` avec :
  - Diagramme d'architecture
  - Sch=C3=A9ma de base de donn=C3=A9es
  - Exemple de collection Postman
- Utilisez [gitmoji](https://gitmoji.dev/) pour des commits plus visuels :
  ```bash
  git commit -m ":sparkles: feat(ai): add auto-compensation system"</pre></=

# Microservice de Hotelna

## =F0=9F=93=8B Description
Notre application de gestion h=C3=B4teli=C3=A8re offre une plateforme compl=
=C3=A8te permettant une administration efficace de l=E2=80=99=C3=A9tablisse=
ment. =20
Ce projet est un microservice d=C3=A9velopp=C3=A9 avec Spring Boot dans le =
cadre d=E2=80=99un syst=C3=A8me distribu=C3=A9. =20
Il est d=C3=A9di=C3=A9 =C3=A0 la gestion des utilisateurs (CRUD, authentifi=
cation, r=C3=A9initialisation du mot de passe via OTP, etc.).

Il fait partie d=E2=80=99une architecture microservices avec :
- Un service Eureka (Service Discovery)
- Un API Gateway (Spring Cloud Gateway)
- D'autres microservices=20

---

## =F0=9F=9B=A0=EF=B8=8F Technologies utilis=C3=A9es

- **Java 17**
- **Spring Boot** (Framework principal)
- **Spring Data JPA** (Pour l'acc=C3=A8s aux donn=C3=A9es)
- **Spring Cloud** (Eureka, Gateway)
- **MySQL** (Base de donn=C3=A9es)
- **Swagger / OpenAPI** (Documentation et test des API)
- **Lombok** (R=C3=A9duction de code boilerplate)
- **Git** (Gestion de version)

---

## =F0=9F=9A=80 Fonctionnalit=C3=A9s

- **CRUD des utilisateurs** (ajout, mise =C3=A0 jour, suppression, consulta=
tion)
- **Authentification via login** (Email + mot de passe)
- **R=C3=A9initialisation du mot de passe par OTP** (Envoi de code par mail=
)
- **Recherche d=E2=80=99utilisateurs par nom**
- **Int=C3=A9gration Swagger pour tester les endpoints** via l'interface we=
b.
- **Communication avec d'autres microservices** via Eureka et Gateway.

---

## =F0=9F=94=A7 Installation

### 1. Cloner le projet
```bash
git clone https://github.com/youssefsayari/hotelna.git
```

### 2. Configurer la base de donn=C3=A9es MySQL

Dans `src/main/resources/application.properties`, configurez la connexion =
=C3=A0 votre base de donn=C3=A9es MySQL :

```properties
spring.datasource.url=3Djdbc:mysql://localhost:3306/hotelna_db
spring.datasource.username=3Droot
spring.datasource.password=3Droot
spring.jpa.hibernate.ddl-auto=3Dupdate
```

### 3. Lancer le projet

Assurez-vous que Maven est install=C3=A9 et ex=C3=A9cutez la commande suiva=
nte pour d=C3=A9marrer le microservice :

```bash
mvn spring-boot:run
```

### 4. Acc=C3=A9der =C3=A0 Swagger

Une fois l'application lanc=C3=A9e, acc=C3=A9dez =C3=A0 Swagger pour tester=
 les endpoints via :

```
http://localhost:8090/swagger-ui/index.html
```

---

## =F0=9F=93=A1 API Endpoints

| M=C3=A9thode | Endpoint                        | Description             =
               |
|---------|----------------------------------|-----------------------------=
-----------|
| GET     | /user/getAllUsers               | R=C3=A9cup=C3=A9rer tous les =
utilisateurs        |
| GET     | /user/getUserById/{id}          | R=C3=A9cup=C3=A9rer un utilis=
ateur par ID        |
| POST    | /user/addUser                   | Ajouter un utilisateur       =
          |
| PUT     | /user/updateUser                | Mettre =C3=A0 jour un utilisa=
teur           |
| DELETE  | /user/deleteUser/{id}           | Supprimer un utilisateur     =
          |
| POST    | /user/login                     | Authentifier un utilisateur  =
          |
| POST    | /user/send-otp                  | Envoyer un OTP pour reset pas=
sword     |
| POST    | /user/verify-otp                | V=C3=A9rifier un OTP         =
               |
| POST    | /user/change-password           | Changer le mot de passe      =
          |
| GET     | /user/search?name=3Dxxxx          | Rechercher par nom         =
            |

---

## =F0=9F=A7=B0 Architecture du projet

Le microservice utilise **Spring Cloud Eureka** pour la d=C3=A9couverte de =
services, et **Spring Cloud Gateway** comme passerelle d'API pour acheminer=
 les demandes vers le service appropri=C3=A9.

**Architecture globale :**
- **Eureka Service** (D=C3=A9couverte de services)
- **API Gateway** (Point d'entr=C3=A9e unifi=C3=A9 pour les microservices)
- **Microservice de gestion des utilisateurs**
- **Autres microservices** (Gestion des missions, cong=C3=A9s, etc.)
 =20
---

## =F0=9F=93=85 Roadmap

- =E2=9C=85 **MVP** : Gestion des utilisateurs (CRUD)
- =F0=9F=9A=A7 **Fonctionnalit=C3=A9s futures** :
  - Authentification via JWT (JSON Web Token)
  - Gestion de r=C3=B4les utilisateurs (admin, user)
  - Int=C3=A9gration d'un service de messagerie pour les notifications
  - Optimisation des performances via cache (ex : Redis)

---

## =F0=9F=93=88 Documentation Swagger / OpenAPI

Le projet est document=C3=A9 avec Swagger. =20
Vous pouvez acc=C3=A9der =C3=A0 la documentation des API via l'interface Sw=
agger =C3=A0 l'adresse suivante une fois l'application lanc=C3=A9e :

```
http://localhost:8090/swagger-ui/index.html
```

---

## =E2=9C=85 Bonnes pratiques Git

- Commits r=C3=A9guliers avec messages explicites et clairs
- Utilisation de branches pour chaque fonctionnalit=C3=A9
- Structure du projet bien d=C3=A9finie
- Mise =C3=A0 jour r=C3=A9guli=C3=A8re du fichier README.md

<span class=3D"token title important"><span class=3D"token punctuation">##<=
/span> =F0=9F=93=8B Description</span>
Module intelligent de gestion des r=C3=A9clamations pour =C3=A9tablissement=
s h=C3=B4teliers int=C3=A9grant : =20
=E2=9C=85 G=C3=A9n=C3=A9ration automatis=C3=A9e de solutions par IA (Mistra=
l AI) =20
=E2=9C=85 Workflow de suivi multi-=C3=A9tats (Ouvert/En cours/R=C3=A9solu/F=
erm=C3=A9) =20
=E2=9C=85 Interface administrateur/visiteur =20

Ce microservice Spring Boot fait partie d'une architecture distribu=C3=A9e =
comprenant : =20
<span class=3D"token list punctuation">-</span> Service Discovery (Eureka S=
erver) =20

ateway) =20
<span class=3D"token list punctuation">-</span> Autres microservices (Utili=
sateurs, R=C3=A9servations...)
